The big reason I won't buy sketches ever again. Even since I buy a pair with this memory foam I'm constantly shocking myself & my co-workers. Never had this problem before & I take my shoes off when I get home & miraculously no more shocking until I put the shoes in. It's so bad you can actually see the shock, people actually tell me they see & hear it even if they are not right by me.  I know it isn't my work environment causing it because it's just me & not my co-workers. Also it happens at home only if my shoes are on.

Since my first pair, never bought anything else since 2000. Now they came out with this memory foam.  Most shoes feel so tight I won't buy them, the sneakers are the only ones that fit & they have to be wide. Wide selection is very minimum.<//review>

< Text>
Long Covid and infection burst a tooth. During the pandemic, many dentists were closed, but SmileSF was taking patients and had good reviews. The diagnosis was to address a variety of issues to give me the best chance of success with a crown on the broken tooth: Gum treatment was needed to clear infection, home care would be required to heal the gums. Next, the broken tooth was flanked by two teeth with old fillings, so those fillings were ready to be replaced, and the best time to do it would be during the clean out and installation of the new crown. I could understand it would be dicey dealing with either of those fillings later. So over the last 6 weeks I've had all this work done. The bonus is that my Long Covid episodes (which had escalated during the few weeks before my tooth burst) have subsided a great deal. Causation or correlation? Who knows? Long Covid is a mystery at this point. But many of us who had Covid-19 are having a variety of dental problems. SmileSF is practicing good protocols to keep them and we safe from re-infection. If you are cohort 2 (as I am) and episodes are increasing, checking for infection of your gums and teeth might be worthwhile. This office is struggling a bit with the Pandemic protocols, as everyone is. But they are fully equipped and careful. I would recommend Dr. Farah Sefidvash.<//Text>

<Text>We have been going to Mona Lisa on Waring Road for 42 year.  This is the best pizza I have ever tasted and I'm from Chicago so I know pizza.  It is a thinner crust than the Chicago pizza but it is amazing.  They spare no amount of cheese and the Italian sausage and pepperoni are the best quality.  Don't know why Americans call it "Italian" sausage because we have been to Italy numerous times and they don't have sausage any where near what we call "American"  Italian sausage.  Salami is what they serve on your pizza in Italy if you want a spicy meat.  So...that being said we go no where else other than Mona Lisa on Waring Road for our pizza.  Yes, it is getting quite pricey but well worth the extra dollars. The guys behind the counter that make the pizza work so hard to make a quality product.  Kudos to them.  The restaurant is quaint and the servers are very friendly.  Our go to place for a great pizza.

<Review>This is my 4th time here. First two times were excellent, burgers and portion of fries were huge, totally worth the price. The first time My son and I got the original burgers (which is not spicy), and my husband and daughter got the hot ones. The second time, me and my son got chicken tenders and husband and daughter the burgers. That time when we got the tenders, they came with a side of pickled radish for the same price of the tenders. The third time, they didn't have chicken tenders but instead they had tacos. Well, that third time wax ver disappointed for my husband and I because the portions were way smaller than previous visits. Before, the burger and fries would barely fit in the cute box they had. That time, nope. We agreed not to come again. But today we were in the area and the kids were hungry and all they wanted was Michindak. Well, here we are. My daughter and I got chicken tenders, they don't give you the pickled radish with the tenders but they sell it separately for $2 extra. My son ordered the burger and it still comes with fries but the burger is tiny (like a McDonald's jr burger) and the portion of fries is like 1/4 of what it used to be. My husband ordered the whole fried chicken, which looks very differently from the picture, but well, nothing impressive for a  $15.99 plus taxes fried chicken. I'm sorry, I loved this place but  every visit is getting worse than the last. Today we told the kids that most likely were never coming back. Worth mentioning that customer service is good, staff is very helpful and nice, that's always gonna be a 5 star but the food is inconsistent in size every time.< /Review>< username>

<userid>103783004263036629672<//userid>< Text>
A friend of mine lives nearby here, and recommended this place while I was visiting. We ordered a couple of chicken burgers, some chicken strips, fries, and a whole pickle.

I forget what exact flavor the chicken strips were, it was the one with the sweet orange sauce. These were excellent. Chicken is cooked wonderfully, juicy on the inside and crispy on the outside.

As for the chicken burgers, we ordered two regular and one hot. For those of you debating what level of spice to get, allow me to provide a warning. Here I was thinking oh, they have 4 or 5 levels of spice, I'm pretty good with spice and don't mind melting my face a little, let's go for level 2 (hot - level 1 is original). I was a fool. Young, naive. So full of hope. First, let me say that this chicken sandwich was amazing. The sliced pickles, the bun, the chicken itself, everything was phenomenal. But oh boy was this sandwich hot. Like, really hot. I couldn't finish it. I almost did, and oh my god I wanted to finish this sandwich, it tasted so good. But I couldn't. I'm definitely coming back for this sandwich, but next time hopefully I'm prepared (someone else said they had theirs with milk, great idea). If that was their hot, I'm sure their next levels of spice beyond that are insane. There's something about this sandwich though, I will definitely willfully subject myself to that torture again for that.

I came back again and got the original chicken burger and fries, and was again amazing (and hey I could easily finish it this time!).

I highly recommend this place and will definitely be coming back.<//Text>

< Text>
A friend of mine lives nearby here, and recommended this place while I was visiting. We ordered a couple of chicken burgers, some chicken strips, fries, and a whole pickle.

I forget what exact flavor the chicken strips were, it was the one with the sweet orange sauce. These were excellent. Chicken is cooked wonderfully, juicy on the inside and crispy on the outside.

As for the chicken burgers, we ordered two regular and one hot. For those of you debating what level of spice to get, allow me to provide a warning. Here I was thinking oh, they have 4 or 5 levels of spice, I'm pretty good with spice and don't mind melting my face a little, let's go for level 2 (hot - level 1 is original). I was a fool. Young, naive. So full of hope. First, let me say that this chicken sandwich was amazing. The sliced pickles, the bun, the chicken itself, everything was phenomenal. But oh boy was this sandwich hot. Like, really hot. I couldn't finish it. I almost did, and oh my god I wanted to finish this sandwich, it tasted so good. But I couldn't. I'm definitely coming back for this sandwich, but next time hopefully I'm prepared (someone else said they had theirs with milk, great idea). If that was their hot, I'm sure their next levels of spice beyond that are insane. There's something about this sandwich though, I will definitely willfully subject myself to that torture again for that.

I came back again and got the original chicken burger and fries, and was again amazing (and hey I could easily finish it this time!).

I highly recommend this place and will definitely be coming back.</Text>

<review>Fried chicken? Love. Heat in my mouth? Double love. A crunchy sandwich? Triple love. All put in the name of Michin Dak? So-so.

I really wanted to fall in love with Michin Dak, but it fell short of love and landed somewhat of mediocre. It isn't that their spicy fried chicken is bad, but... When I took my first bite, the bun was mushy. The flavor was spicy and on the spot, but the fries were unforgivably horrible. I took a bite and the rest went into a trash can.

I also had their macaroni salad and it was... naw at best. Given that the flavor of the sandwich was on the spot, I may give it another try. Until then, this barely three-star review remains.

<text>The Place: This took over the old dumpling place. You're going to a hut and eating outside. I actually would like to see more of these types of places given the mild weather LA has.

The Food: The chicken was amazing. Some of the best fried chicken sandwiches I have had. Their medium spicy is more on the hot side compared to what other places consider medium (which makes sense, they are specializing in spicy chicken). For me the medium was that perfect balance of heat but still could taste the other flavors. The Cole Slaw on the sandwich was nice and cooling. However, my complaint is that their fries are just "meh." Also when we got to the bottom of the popcorn chicken the sauce got too concentrated and was way too sweet for us. It was still good but just be mindful that the bottom may bring disappointment.

Pricing: Pricing is on par for the neighborhood. It may be more pricey than fast food, but unlike fast food you won't have regrets (unless you're sensitive to spicy food) an hour later. I will say their iced peach tea was overpriced. I would stick with the soda or bottled water if you're eating there. The iced tea was good, but was not worth the price. If it was a $1 or $1.50, it would be worth it.

What I Would Like Changed: They should get rid of the steak fries and offer tater tots or shoe-string fries. Honestly their fries were disappointing, not as disappointing as In-N-Out fries but almost as bad. Also as stated in pricing, they should lower the price of the iced tea. I get they have a nice mark-up and can make a good profit on it, but it left us feeling a little ripped off given the $3 price tag.< /text><rate>5<//rate>< pics>
None< /pics>

<time>1590642317276< /time><Rating>1< /Rating>< text>
i bought a 24' Coleman Lantern camping trailer last June, 2019, hoping to have a great camping season.  It spent most of the summer and fall in the shop with multiple repairs and issues with systems not working, waiting for parts or authorization to work on it, or just in the Que waiting for my turn.  We went camping twice.  I finally got it back in late November.  Wow!! What a bad experience.  I would not wish this on anyone.  Here's some examples, 1.  The water tanks would not fill initially and only allowed 10 gallons of water into the tanks.  A pinched vent line was the culprit.  2.  The leveling jack in the rear of the trailer would only extend one side.  3.  The panel above the master bed was riddled with staples and had to be replaced, 4.  The light above the stove did not work, 5. The refrigerator would not cool down below 50 degrees, 6.  The window near the bunks had a bent arm brace and would not hold the window open, 7.  The panels in the bathroom were not secured to the wood framing and even now are not repaired properly.  8.  Staples are hanging out and not fully shot into the wood framing so they catch you when you walk by, 9.  The rubber seal around the slide out is ripped and torn.  Most of these items were repaired.  This spring I noticed the framing in the front storage area had a broken board hanging down since it had a large knot in it and one of the other boards was never fastened properly.  I'm not taking it back to get worked on unless I have to.  I repaired it myself.  I wish we had never purchased the trailer but maybe this year will be better....We do like the layout of the trailer and hope it's not a lemon.  Buyer beware.  Do a thorough inspection before picking up the trailer.  Don't let them rush you out or only give you a few minutes to review everything.  Take your time!!<//text>

<Gmap_id>0x809b2074b91950f9:0xacb6b6fd1b48f9bf</Gmap_id>< Text>
In my 20 years of RVing, and 4 RVs, my experience with this dealership is the worst I've ever had. It took 3 trips and weeks of delays to have an electrical outlet repaired. Each time they fix the perceived problem, but do not check their work, resulting in scheduling yet another service.

Shortly after purchasing my RV I discovered that the air vent in the roof behind the driver seat was installed backward! Driving with the hatch open would have caused the lid to blow off. Quality Control??

After discovering a leak in a storage hatch perimeter, they caulked around it. Next rain.... the adjacent hatch perimeter leaked.... they did not bother to caulk the second one.

After driving in a sustained rain, water ponded in the middle of the RV floor. After they supposedly fixed it, the leak reappeared in the next rain.

I would caution anyone buying an RV to avoid this dealership if you plan on having your warranty repair work done there.

I give up on these people and will never make another purchase there. I have had good experience with Camping World in Rocklin (I assume a franchise owned by a more capable franchisee), but that franchise cannot do warranty work  on my RV, I assume because I did not buy it from them.<//Text>
